msg:This is a hotel with both positives and negatives. Overall, it can score 3.5-4 points.

Let me talk about the advantages first: the location of the hotel is very good, in the most prosperous area of Wujiaochang, exit No. 5 of the subway station, it takes about 5 or 6 minutes to walk to the hotel, or you can go directly to the hotel through Heshenghui. The nearby commercial center has a complete range of dining and entertainment, with a variety of choices, so eating and shopping is not a problem. The size of the hotel room is acceptable, very clean, without any peculiar smell. The toilet and small cloakroom are designed in one, which is very user-friendly and convenient. The service attitude of the staff is very good. The front desk, cafeteria, and room cleaning that I have contacted with are mostly very good and responsive to requests. The breakfast is quite satisfactory, there are no highlights, but it is not out of standard. Also, the robots that shuttle hotel services are cute.

Let's talk about the disadvantages: the biggest disadvantage is that the room is too noisy. The room I was given at the beginning was just facing the Central Elevated Road, and the noise was very loud. When I was in the room, it felt like I was on the street. Later, I changed to another room, still a little bit facing Central, and the noise was almost the same as the first room. Unwilling to make a fuss, I stayed. As a result, I didn't sleep well for two nights, and the noise was constant 24 hours a day. The second problem is that the room is too hot. Probably because of energy saving, the hotel's air conditioner is not cooling, because the room faces southwest, and the room temperature in the afternoon can reach 28,9 degrees. Reluctantly asked to open the window, but there was more noise when the window was opened.

The air conditioning problem is acceptable. If you are not in the room during the day, the room temperature will basically drop at night. But the noise problem, I hope the hotel can seriously consider and solve it, otherwise it is really a big flaw.
